### <a id="the-inductive-types-h-s-p-v">The Inductive Types H, S, P, V</a>

This section presents the [Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="329" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="333" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="341" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="367" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="374" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="379" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="384" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="391" href="Algebras.Signatures.html" class="Module">Algebras.Signatures</a> <a id="411" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="418" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1238" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="427" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="429" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#8157" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="430" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="432" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="433" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="435" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="440" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="447" href="Universes.html" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="457" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="464" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="472" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="474" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">_̇</a><a id="476" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="479" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="506" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="507" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="509" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="511" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1238" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="521" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#8157" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="523" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="524" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="526" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝓧</a> <a id="528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="530" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="538" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="540" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="544" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝓧</a> <a id="546" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="547" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="549" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="556" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="561" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="568" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">Varieties.EquationalLogic</a> <a id="594" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="595" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="597" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="599" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="600" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="602" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝓧</a><a id="603" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="605" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">X</a><a id="606" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="608" class="Keyword">public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3543" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3548" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3550" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3551" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3989" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3991" href="Algebras.Products.html#1145" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="3993" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3940" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="3995" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3997" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3999" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3567" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="P.pisou"></a><a id="4002" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4002" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a>  <a id="4009" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4011" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4012" <a id="4043" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4044" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4046" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4048" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4012" id="4058" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4060" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3567" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4062" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4064" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4012" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4072" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4029" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4074" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4076"  <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4081" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4081" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4088" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4090" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4091" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4091" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4093" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4093" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4095" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4097" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4105" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4107" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4108" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4110" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4112" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4091" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4114" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4116" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4117" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4118" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3551" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4119" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4121" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3553" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4122" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4124" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3567" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4126" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4128" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4091" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4130" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#961" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4132" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4093" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4134" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4136" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4093" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4138" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4140" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4142" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3567" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4482" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4487" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4489" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4490" <a id="4510" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="4514" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4515" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4523" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="5090" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5092" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5092" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5094" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5096" <a id="5110" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5111" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5113" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5115" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="5118" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5118" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5120" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5123" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5092" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5125" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5118" class="Bound">i</a><a id="5126" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5128" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5130" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5131" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5132" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4490" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5133" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5135" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4492" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5136" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5138" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="5139" id="5147" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5149" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5151" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5154" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5154" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5161" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5163" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5164" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5164" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5166" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5168" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5176" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4490" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5178" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5179" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5181" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5181" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5183" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5185" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5193" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5195" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5196" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5198" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5200" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5164" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5202" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5204" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5205" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5206" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4490" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5207" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5209" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4490" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5210" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5212" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5214" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5216" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5164" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5218" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#961" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5220" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5181" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5222" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5224" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5181" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5226" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5228" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5230" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5233" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5242" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5243" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5243" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5245" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5249" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5257" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5259" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5260" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5262" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5264" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5243" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5266" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5268" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5269" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5270" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4490" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5271" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5273" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4492" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5274" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5276" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5278" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5280" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5243" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5282" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#961" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5284" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5286" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5288" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5290" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5292" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5294" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4506" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5646" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5646" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5657" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5659" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5660" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5660" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5662" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5664" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5672" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5674" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5674" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5676" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5678" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5683" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5684" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5692" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5660" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5694" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5695" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5697" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5700" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5660" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5701" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5704" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5706" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5709" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5660" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5711" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5713" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5646" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5723" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5724" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5724" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5725" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5729" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5731" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5732" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5733" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5724" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5734" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5736" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5724" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5737" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5739" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5741" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2587" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5743" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5746" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5746" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5754" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5756" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5757" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5757" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5759" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5761" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5769" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5771" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5773" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5774" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5777" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5757" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5778" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5779" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5781" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5783" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5746" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5791" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5791" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5793" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5795" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5797" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5797" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5799" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5801" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5802" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5808" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5816" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5791" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5818" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5819" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5821" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5791" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5825" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5828" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5830" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5646" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5841" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5797" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P-mono"></a><a id="6273" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6273" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="6280" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6282" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6283" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6283" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6285" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6285" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="6287" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6289" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6297" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6299" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6299" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6301" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6301" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="6304" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6306" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="6310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6311" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6319" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6283" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6321" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6322" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6324" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6327" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6283" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6328" class="Symbol">)}</a>

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S-mono"></a><a id="7554" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7554" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7561" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7563" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7564" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7564" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7566" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7566" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="7568" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7570" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="7578" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7580" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7580" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7582" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7582" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="7585" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7587" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="7592" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7593" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="7601" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7564" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7603" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="7604" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="7606" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="7609" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7564" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7610" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="7614" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="7622" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7580" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7624" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2587" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="7626" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7582" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="7629" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7631" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2859" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="7632" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7633" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7564" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7634" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7636" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7566" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7637" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7639" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7580" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7641" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2587" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="7643" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2859" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="7644" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7645" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7564" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7646" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7648" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7566" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7649" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7651" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7582" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a>

<a id="7655" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7554" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7662" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7662" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7666" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7667" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2950" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="7673" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7673" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7674" class="Symbol">)</a>            <a id="7687" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7689" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2950" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="7695" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7696" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7662" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7700" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7673" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7701" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="7758" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7554" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7765" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7765" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7769" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7770" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3070" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="7774" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7775" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7776" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7778" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7778" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7779" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7781" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="7784" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7784" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="7787" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="7790" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7792" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3070" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="7797" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7798" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7554" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7765" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7809" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7781" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="7811" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7784" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="7817" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7554" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7824" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7828" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7829" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3148" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="7834" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7835" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7835" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7836" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7838" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7838" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7839" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7841" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7841" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="7844" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7844" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="7847" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7849" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7851" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3148" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="7857" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7858" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7554" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7865" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7824" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7869" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7841" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="7871" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7873" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7844" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="7877" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7554" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7884" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7884" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7889" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3211" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7894" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7894" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7896" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7896" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7898" class="Symbol">)</a>          <a id="7909" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7911" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3211" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7917" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7554" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7924" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7884" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7928" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7894" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7929" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7931" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7896" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="8143" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8150" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8150" class="Module">_</a> <a id="8152" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8153" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8153" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8155" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8155" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8157" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8159" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8167" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8169" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8169" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8171" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8173" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8178" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8179" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8187" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8153" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8189" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8190" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8192" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8195" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8153" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8196" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8199" class="Keyword">where</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">
<a id="10138" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10145" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10145" class="Module">_</a> <a id="10147" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10148" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10148" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10150" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10150" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10152" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10154" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="10162" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10164" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10164" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10166" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10168" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10173" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10174" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10182" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10148" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10184" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10185" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10187" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10190" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10148" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10191" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="10194" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="10202" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10202" class="Function">Lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="10216" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10218" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10219" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10221" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10223" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10231" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10148" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10233" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10234" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="10238" class="Symbol">→</a>              <a id="10253" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10219" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10255" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4785" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10275" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10276" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="10277" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10278" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10148" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10279" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10281" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10148" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10282" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10284" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10164" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="10285" class="Symbol">)</a>
                 <a id="10304" class="Comment">-------------------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="10356" class="Symbol">→</a>              <a id="10371" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10372" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4135" class="Function">Lift-alg</a> <a id="10381" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10219" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10383" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10150" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10384" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10386" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4785" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10406" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10407" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="10408" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10409" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10148" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10410" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10412" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10150" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10413" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10415" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10164" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="10416" class="Symbol">)</a>

   <a id="10664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10646" class="Function">plA</a> <a id="10668" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10670" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3696" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftu</a> <a id="10677" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10454" class="Bound">pA</a>

</pre>

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

  <a id="13416" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13400" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="13418" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13420" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3838" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="13426" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13429" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13429" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13431" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13433" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6725" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="13440" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13441" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13759" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="13443" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13815" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="13447" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13811" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13449" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12755" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="13453" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13429" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13455" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13811" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13457" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13759" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="13458" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="13674" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="13681" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13681" class="Module">_</a> <a id="13683" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13684" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13684" class="Bound">fovu</a> <a id="13689" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13691" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2039" class="Function">dfunext</a> <a id="13699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13700" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13703" href="Universes.html#260" class="Generalizable">𝓤</a><a id="13704" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13707" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13710" href="Universes.html#260" class="Generalizable">𝓤</a><a id="13711" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="13714" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13714" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="13716" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13718" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="13723" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13724" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="13732" href="Universes.html#260" class="Generalizable">𝓤</a> <a id="13734" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="13735" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="13737" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13740" href="Universes.html#260" class="Generalizable">𝓤</a><a id="13741" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13744" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="13752" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13752" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="13758" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13760" class="Comment">-- extensionality assumptions:</a>
            <a id="13803" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="13811" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13812" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13815" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13703" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13816" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="13818" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13821" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13703" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13822" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13827" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="13834" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="13835" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13836" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231"  <a id="14948" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13752" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="14954" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14954" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14959" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4081" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a><a id="14964" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14965" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14965" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="14966" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14968" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14968" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="14969" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14971" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14971" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="14974" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14974" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="14977" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14979" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14981" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3211" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="14986" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14987" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#13752" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="14993" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14954" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14997" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14971" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="14999" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15001" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14974" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an algebra 𝑨 belongs to the variety V 𝒦, then so does the lift of 𝑨.  Let us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="16377" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="16382" href="Overture.Lifts.html#2467" class="Module">Lift</a>

<a id="16388" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Vlift"></a><a id="16395" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16395" class="Module">Vlift</a> <a id="16401" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16402" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16402" class="Bound">fe₀</a> <a id="16406" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16408" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2039" class="Function">dfunext</a> <a id="16416" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16417" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16420" href="Universes.html#260" class="Generalizable">𝓤</a><a id="16421" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16423" href="Universes.html#260" class="Generalizable">𝓤</a><a id="16424" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="17398" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17359" class="Function">B≅A</a> <a id="17402" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17404" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5632" class="Function">Lift-alg-⨅≅</a>  <a id="17417" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17418" class="Argument">fizw</a> <a id="17423" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16436" class="Bound">fe₁</a><a id="17428" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17430" class="Argument">fiu</a> <a id="17434" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17436" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16402" class="Bound">fe₀</a><a id="17439" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17441" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17287" class="Function">iso-components</a>


 <a id="17459" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16570" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="17463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17464" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5073" class="InductiveConstructor">vprodw</a><a id="17470" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17471" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17471" class="Bound">I</a><a id="17472" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17474" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17474" class="Bound">𝒜</a><a id="17475" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17477" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17477" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17478" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17480" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17482" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17489" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5073" class="InductiveConstructor">vprodw</a> <a id="17496" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17626" class="Function">vlA</a><a id="17499" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17501" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17502" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1560" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="17508" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17765" class="Function">B≅A</a><a id="17511" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="17515" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="17523" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17523" class="Function">𝑰</a> <a id="17525" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17527" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17528" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17531" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16420" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17533" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="17534" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17536" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
  <a id="17540" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17523" class="Function">𝑰</a> <a id="17542" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17544" href="Overture.Lifts.html#2467" class="Record">Lift</a> <a id="17549" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17471" class="Bound">I</a>

  <a id="17554" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17554" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="17557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17559" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17523" class="Function">𝑰</a> <a id="17561" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17563" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17572" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17575" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16420" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17577" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="17578" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17580" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
  <a id="17584" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17554" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="17587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17587" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="17589" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17591" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4135" class="Function">Lift-alg</a> <a id="17600" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17601" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17474" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="17603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17604" href="Overture.Lifts.html#2541" class="Field">lower</a> <a id="17610" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17587" class="Bound">i</a><a id="17611" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="17614" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17615" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17618" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16420" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17620" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="17621" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="17626" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17626" class="Function">vlA</a> <a id="17630" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17632" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="17634" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17634" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="17636" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17639" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17554" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="17642" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17634" class="Bound">i</a><a id="17643" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17645" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="17647" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4487" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="17648" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17649" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16420" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17650" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17652" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17655" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16420" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17657" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="17658" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17660" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16532" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="17693" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17693" class="Function">iso-components</a> <a id="17708" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17710" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="17712" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17712" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="17714" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17716" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17474" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="17718" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17712" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="17720" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#961" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="17722" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17554" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="17725" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17726" href="Overture.Lifts.html#2529" class="InductiveConstructor">lift</a> <a id="17731" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17712" class="Bound">i</a><a id="17732" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="17736" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17693" class="Function">iso-components</a> <a id="17751" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17751" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="17753" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17755" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2754" class="Function">Lift-≅</a>

  <a id="17765" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17765" class="Function">B≅A</a> <a id="17769" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17771" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4135" class="Function">Lift-alg</a> <a id="17780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17781" href="Algebras.Products.html#1145" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="17783" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17474" class="Bound">𝒜</a><a id="17784" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17787" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17790" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16420" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17792" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="17793" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17795" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#961" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="17797" href="Algebras.Products.html#1145" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="17799" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17554" class="Function">lA</a>
  <a id="17804" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17765" class="Function">B≅A</a> <a id="17808" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17810" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5632" class="Function">Lift-alg-⨅≅</a> <a id="17822" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17823" class="Argument">fizw</a> <a id="17828" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17830" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16436" class="Bound">fe₁</a><a id="17833" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17835" class="Argument">fiu</a> <a id="17839" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17841" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16493" class="Bound">fe₂</a><a id="17844" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17846" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17693" class="Function">iso-components</a>

 <a id="17863" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16570" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="17867" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17868" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5154" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a><a id="17873" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17874" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17874" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17875" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17877" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17877" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17878" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17880" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17880" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17882" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17882" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="17885" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17887" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17889" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17895" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17896" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4635" class="InductiveConstructor">vlift</a> <a id="17902" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17880" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17903" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17905" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17906" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3386" class="Function">Lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="17919" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17882" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="17922" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="17925" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16570" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="17929" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17930" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a><a id="17935" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17936" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17936" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17937" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17939" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17939" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17940" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17942" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17942" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17944" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17944" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="17947" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17949" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17951" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17957" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17958" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16570" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="17962" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17942" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17963" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17966" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3386" class="Function">Lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="17979" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17944" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="17982" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>



Above we proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="18324" class="Comment">-- module _ {𝒦 : Pred (Algebra 𝓤 𝑆) (ov 𝓤)} where</a>

 <a id="18423" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18376" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18429" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18430" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2950" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="18435" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18436" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18436" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18437" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18439" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18439" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18440" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18442" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18444" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18450" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18451" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16570" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18455" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18456" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15593" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18461" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18462" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2950" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="18468" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18439" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18469" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="18473" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18474" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1560" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="18480" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18481" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4041" class="Function">Lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="18502" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18436" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18503" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="18600" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="18714" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18376" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18720" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18721" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3211" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a><a id="18725" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18726" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18726" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18727" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18729" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18729" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18730" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18732" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18732" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18734" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18734" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="18737" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18739" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18741" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5233" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18747" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18748" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16570" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18752" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18753" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15593" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18758" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18732" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18759" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18762" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18775" class="Function">γ</a>
  <a id="18766" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18775" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18777" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18779" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4135" class="Function">Lift-alg</a> <a id="18788" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18726" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18790" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18791" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18794" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16420" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18796" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18797" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18799" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#961" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="18801" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18729" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
   <a id="18806" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18775" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18808" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18810" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1738" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="18818" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18819" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1560" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="18825" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2754" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="18831" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18833" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18734" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

Before doing so, we need to redefine the class product so that each factor comes with a map from the type `X` of variable symbols into that factor.  We will explain the reason for this below.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19526" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-products-with-maps"></a><a id="19533" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19533" class="Module">class-products-with-maps</a>
 <a id="19559" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19560" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19562" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19564" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19572" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19574" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19574" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19576" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19578" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19580" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="19581" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="19584" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19585" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19585" class="Bound">fe₀</a> <a id="19589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19591" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2039" class="Function">dfunext</a> <a id="19599" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19600" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19603" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19604" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19606" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19607" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="19610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19611" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19611" class="Bound">fe₁</a> <a id="19615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19617" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2039" class="Function">dfunext</a> <a id="19625" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="19627" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19630" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19631" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19633" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="19635" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="19637" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19640" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19641" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="19642" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="19643" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19646" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="19648" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19651" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19652" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19654" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="19655" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="19659" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19660" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19660" class="Bound">fe₂</a> <a id="19664" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19666" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2039" class="Function">dfunext</a> <a id="19674" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19675" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19678" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19679" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19681" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19682" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19686" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="19690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19691" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19691" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19693" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19695" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1534" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19700" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19701" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19709" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19711" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19712" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19714" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19717" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19718" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="19722" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.ℑ"></a><a id="19730" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19730" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19732" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19734" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19737" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19739" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="19742" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19730" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19744" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19746" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="19748" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19748" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19750" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="19752" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19753" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19761" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19763" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19764" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19766" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="19768" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19769" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19748" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19771" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19773" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2859" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="19774" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19776" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19778" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19779" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19691" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19782" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19784" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3515" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="19786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19787" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19574" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19789" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19791" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13759" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="19793" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19748" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19795" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13759" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="19796" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>
Notice that the second component of this dependent pair type is  `(𝑨 ∈ 𝒦) × (X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣)`. In previous versions of the [UALib][] this second component was simply `𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, until we realized that adding the type `X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣` is quite useful. Later we will see exactly why, but for now suffice it to say that a map of type `X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣` may be viewed abstractly as an *ambient context*, or more concretely, as an assignment of *values* in `∣ 𝑨 ∣` to *variable symbols* in `X`.  When computing with or reasoning about products, while we don't want to rigidly impose a context in advance, want do want to lay our hands on whatever context is ultimately assumed.  Including the "context map" inside the index type `ℑ` of the product turns out to be a convenient way to achieve this flexibility.


Taking the product over the index type ℑ requires a function that maps an index `i : ℑ` to the corresponding algebra.  Each `i : ℑ` is a triple, say, `(𝑨 , p , h)`, where `𝑨 : Algebra 𝓤 𝑆`, `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, and `h : X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`, so the function mapping an index to the corresponding algebra is simply the first projection.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.𝔄"></a><a id="20931" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20931" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="20933" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20935" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19730" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="20937" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20939" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20947" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20949" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="20952" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20931" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="20954" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20956" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="20958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20959" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20959" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="20961" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20963" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19730" class="Function">ℑ</a><a id="20964" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20966" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20968" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13759" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="20970" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20959" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="20972" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13759" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Finally, we define `class-product` which represents the product of all members of 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-product"></a><a id="21088" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21088" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21102" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21104" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="21112" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21113" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21116" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21117" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21119" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="21122" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21088" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21136" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21138" href="Algebras.Products.html#1145" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="21140" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20931" class="Function">𝔄</a>

</pre>

If `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦` and `h : X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`, we view the triple `(𝑨 , p , h) ∈ ℑ` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p , h)` (which is simply `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ 𝔄` onto the `(𝑨 , p, h)`-th component.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="21408" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21408" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="21426" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21428" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21088" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21442" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21444" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="21445" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21446" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21449" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21450" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21452" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21455" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21456" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="21458" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2859" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="21460" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19691" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21461" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="21464" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21408" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="21482" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21484" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4002" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="21490" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21761" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="21497" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21498" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4524" class="Function">⨅≅</a><a id="21500" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21501" class="Argument">fiw</a> <a id="21505" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21507" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19585" class="Bound">fe₀</a><a id="21510" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21512" class="Argument">fiu</a> <a id="21516" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21518" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19660" class="Bound">fe₂</a><a id="21521" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21523" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21812" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="21528" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="21532" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="21540" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21540" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="21543" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21543" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21547" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21549" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19730" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="21551" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21553" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#844" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="21561" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21562" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21565" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21566" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21568" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#507" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
  <a id="21572" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21540" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="21575" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21575" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21577" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="21580" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4135" class="Function">Lift-alg</a> <a id="21589" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21590" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20931" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="21592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21575" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21593" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21596" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21599" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21600" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="21604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21543" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21608" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21608" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21610" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21612" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4135" class="Function">Lift-alg</a> <a id="21621" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21622" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21540" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="21625" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21608" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21626" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21628" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21629" href="Algebras.Products.html#2231" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="21632" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21633" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="21638" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21638" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="21642" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21644" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21646" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21646" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21648" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21651" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21540" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="21654" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21646" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21655" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21657" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21659" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2859" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="21661" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19691" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="21665" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21638" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="21669" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21669" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21671" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21673" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3211" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="21678" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21679" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13763" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="21683" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13811" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="21685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21669" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21687" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#13811" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="21688" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21690" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2754" class="Function">Lift-≅</a>

  <a id="21700" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21700" class="Function">psllA</a> <a id="21706" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21708" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21710" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21710" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21712" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21714" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21715" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21543" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21719" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21710" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21720" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21722" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21724" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="21726" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2859" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="21729" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19691" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21730" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="21734" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21700" class="Function">psllA</a> <a id="21740" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21740" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21742" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21744" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3639" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="21750" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21751" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21638" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="21755" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21740" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21756" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="21761" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21761" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="21768" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21770" href="Algebras.Products.html#1145" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="21772" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21543" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21776" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2402" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21778" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3548" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="21780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2859" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="21783" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19691" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21784" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="21788" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21761" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="21795" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21797" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3838" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="21803" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21700" class="Function">psllA</a>

  <a id="21812" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21812" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="21818" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21820" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21822" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21822" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21824" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21826" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21827" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21543" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21831" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21822" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21832" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21834" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#961" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="21836" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21837" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20931" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="21839" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21822" class="Bound">i</a><a id="21840" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="21844" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21812" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="21850" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#21850" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="21852" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21854" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1738" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="21862" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21863" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1560" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="21869" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2754" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="21875" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="21877" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1560" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="21883" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2754" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="21889" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

So, since `PS⊆SP`, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class `𝒦` belongs to `SP(𝒦)`.
